class="link" href="/app-kit">App Kit</a> includes the Bridge capability that lets you move USDC
across blockchains in a few lines of code. It abstracts the underlying
<a href="https://developers.circle.com/cctp" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">CCTP</a> flow so you can bridge without
orchestrating the low-level burn, attestation, and mint steps yourself.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="quick-look"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#quick-look" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Quick look</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">This code snippet bridges between an EVM and non-EVM chain in a single method
call:</span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">});</span></span>

<span data-as="p">For a complete end-to-end flow, follow the
<a class="link" href="/app-kit/quickstarts/bridge-tokens-across-blockchains">quickstart</a>.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="installation"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#installation" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Installation</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">App Kit comes with the Bridge capability installed by default. If you’ve already
<a class="link" href="/app-kit/tutorials/installation">installed App Kit</a>, you can skip this section.
If you only need to bridge and don’t want the full App Kit, you can follow the
steps below to install just the Bridge package.</span>
<span data-as="p">Install the Bridge package and the adapter that matches your environment:</span>

process.exit(1);\n  }\n}\n\nfunction generateMDX(project) {\n  // Collect all types we need to document\n  const typeRegistry = new Map();\n\n  // Find AppKit class\n  const appKit = findByNameAndKind(project, 'AppKit', 128); // 128 = Class\n\n  if (!appKit) {\n    console.error('❌ AppKit class not found');\n    process.exit(1);\n  }\n\n  // Build type registry from method signatures\n  collectTypesFromClass(appKit, typeRegistry, project);\n\n  // Also collect types exposed by the unifiedBalance namespace class\n  const appKitUnifiedBalance = findByNameAndKind(project, 'AppKitUnifiedBalance', 128); // 128 = Class\n  if (appKitUnifiedBalance) {\n    collectTypesFromClass(appKitUnifiedBalance, typeRegistry, project);\n  }\n\n  // Second pass: force-collect nested types that are exported but not directly\n  // referenced in method signatures (e.g., types within union types or nested properties)\n  // Note: These need explicit collection because they're either nested within other types\n  // or re-exported in a way that TypeDoc doesn't automatically traverse\n  const additionalExportedTypes = [\n    { name: 'CCTPSplitConfig', kind: 256 },  // Interface\n    { name: 'CCTPMergedConfig', kind: 256 },  // Interface\n    { name: 'BaseChainDefinition', kind: 256 },  // Interface\n    { name: 'TokenInfo', kind: 256 }  // Interface\n  ];\n\n  for (const typeSpec of additionalExportedTypes) {\n    const typeName = typeSpec.name;\n    const typeKind = typeSpec.kind;\n\n    if (!typeRegistry.has(typeName)) {\n      // Look for the specific kind (e.g., interface vs type alias)\n      const typeNode = findByNameAndKind(project, typeName, typeKind);\n      if (typeNode) {\n        typeRegistry.set(typeName, typeNode);\n        // Recursively collect types referenced by this type\n        if (typeNode.children) {\n          for (const child of typeNode.children) {\n            if (child.type) {\n              collectTypeReferences(child.type, typeRegistry, project);\n            }\n          }\n        }\n        if (typeNode.type) {\n          collectTypeReferences(typeNode.type, typeRegistry, project);\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Start generating MDX\n  let mdx = generateHeader();\n\n  // AppKit Class section\n  mdx += generateAppKitClass(appKit, typeRegistry);\n\n  // Methods section - returns set of types that were nested under methods\n  const methods = appKit.children?.filter(c =\u003e c.kind === 2048 \u0026\u0026 !c.flags?.isPrivate) || [];\n  const nestedTypes = new Set();\n  mdx += generateMethods(methods, typeRegistry, nestedTypes);\n\n  // unifiedBalance namespace section\n  if (appKitUnifiedBalance) {\n    mdx += generateUnifiedBalanceSection(appKitUnifiedBalance, typeRegistry, nestedTypes);\n  }\n\n  // Type sections - exclude nested types\n  mdx += generateTypeSections(typeRegistry, nestedTypes);\n\n  // Event Types section\n  mdx += generateEventTypes(appKit);\n\n  return mdx;\n}\n\nfunction generateHeader() {\n  const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();\n  return `---\ntitle: \"App Kit SDK Reference\"\nsidebarTitle: \"SDK Reference\"\ndescription: \"API reference for App Kit's public interfaces, methods, and types\"\n---\n\n{/* Auto-generated on ${timestamp} by scripts/generate_sdk_reference.js */}\n{/* Do not edit this file directly - regenerate using: yarn sdk-gen */}\n{/* \u003c!-- markdownlint-disable MD036 --\u003e */}\n\nThis reference guide describes the public interfaces, methods, and types\navailable in the App Kit SDK.\n\n`;\n}\n\nfunction generateAppKitClass(appKit, typeRegistry) {\n  let mdx = `## AppKit Class\\n\\n`;\n\n  mdx += `The \\`AppKit\\` is how you'll perform all stablecoin operations including\\n`;\n  mdx += `crosschain bridging, same-chain swaps, token transfers, and fee estimation. It\\n`;\n  mdx += `also enables you to add event listeners for bridge transfers.\\n\\n`;\n\n  // Constructor\n  const constructor = appKit.children?.find(c =\u003e c.name === 'constructor');\n  if (constructor) {\n    mdx += generateConstructor(constructor, typeRegistry);\n  }\n\n  // AppKitConfig type (defined in AppKit.ts)\n  const configType = typeRegistry.get('AppKitConfig');\n  if (configType) {\n    mdx += generateTypeDefinition(configType, 'AppKitConfig');\n  }\n\n  mdx += `---\\n\\n`;\n  return mdx;\n}\n\nfunction generateConstructor(constructor, typeRegistry) {\n  let mdx = `### constructor(config?)\\n\\n`;\n  mdx += `Creates a new \\`AppKit\\` instance.\\n\\n`;\n  mdx += `\\`\\`\\`typescript\\n`;\n  mdx += `constructor(config?: AppKitConfig)\\n`;\n  mdx += `\\`\\`\\`\\n\\n`;\n\n  const sig = constructor.signatures?.[0];\n  if (sig?.parameters) {\n    mdx += `**Parameters**\\n\\n`;\n    mdx += `| Name   | Type                          | Description                                                         |\\n`;\n    mdx += `| ------ | ----------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------- |\\n`;\n    for (const param of sig.parameters) {\n      const typeName = getTypeString(param.type);\n      // Extract base type name without generics for linking\n      const baseTypeName = typeName.split('\u003c')[0].split(' ')[0].replace(/\\\\?\\|/g, '').trim();\n      // Only create link if the type exists in registry\n      const shouldLink = typeRegistry \u0026\u0026 typeRegistry.has(baseTypeName) \u0026\u0026\n                        baseTypeName.length \u003e 1 \u0026\u0026\n                        !typeName.includes('=\u003e');\n      const typeDisplay = shouldLink\n        ? `[\\`${typeName}\\`](#${slugify(baseTypeName)})`\n        : `\\`${typeName}\\``;\n      const desc = cleanDescription(getCommentText(param.comment?.summary), true);\n      mdx += `| ${param.name} | ${typeDisplay} | ${desc} |\\n`;\n    }\n    mdx += `\\n`;\n  }\n\n  const examples = getExamples(sig);\n  if (examples.length \u003e 0) {\n    mdx += `**Usage**\\n\\n`;\n    examples.forEach(example =\u003e {\n      mdx += `\\`\\`\\`typescript\\n${example}\\n\\`\\`\\`\\n\\n`;\n    });\n  }\n\n  return mdx;\n}\n\nfunction generateMethods(methods, typeRegistry, nestedTypes, sectionTitle = 'Methods') {\n  let mdx = `## ${sectionTitle}\\n\\n`;\n\n  // Track how many times each type has been used to generate correct anchor links\n  const typeOccurrences = new Map();\n\n  for (const method of methods) {\n    const sig = method.signatures?.[0];\n    if (!sig) continue;\n\n    // Build parameter list for method signature\n    const paramList = sig.parameters?.map(p =\u003e {\n      const pName = p.name;\n      const pType = getTypeString(p.type);\n      return `${pName}: ${pType}`;\n    }).join(', ') || '';\n\n    // Method heading with just the first parameter name (simplified for heading)\n    const firstParam = sig.parameters?.[0];\n    const headingParam = firstParam ? firstParam.name : '';\n\n    mdx += `### ${method.name}(${headingParam})\\n\\n`;\n\n    // Description\n    const desc = cleanDescription(getCommentText(sig.comment?.summary));\n    if (desc) {\n      mdx += `${desc}\\n\\n`;\n    }\n\n    // Signature\n    mdx += `\\`\\`\\`typescript\\n`;\n    const returnType = getTypeString(sig.type);\n    const isAsync = sig.type?.type === 'reference' \u0026\u0026 sig.type?.name === 'Promise';\n    mdx += `${isAsync ? 'async ' : ''}${method.name}(${paramList}): ${returnType}\\n`;\n    mdx += `\\`\\`\\`\\n\\n`;\n\n    // Parameters table\n    if (sig.parameters \u0026\u0026 sig.parameters.length \u003e 0) {\n      mdx += `**Parameters**\\n\\n`;\n      mdx += `| Name   | Type                          | Description                |\\n`;\n      mdx += `| ------ | ----------------------------- | -------------------------- |\\n`;\n      for (const param of sig.parameters) {\n        const typeName = getTypeString(param.type);\n        // Extract base type name without generics for linking\n        const baseTypeName = typeName.split('\u003c')[0].split(' ')[0].replace(/\\\\?\\|/g, '').trim();\n        // Only create link if the type exists in registry and isn't a generic parameter or function signature\n        const shouldLink = typeRegistry \u0026\u0026 typeRegistry.has(baseTypeName) \u0026\u0026\n                          baseTypeName.length \u003e 1 \u0026\u0026\n                          !typeName.includes('=\u003e') \u0026\u0026\n                          !isGenericType(baseTypeName);\n        // Strip generics from display but keep base type\n        const displayTypeName = baseTypeName;\n        // Calculate the occurrence number for this type\n        const occurrenceCount = typeOccurrences.get(baseTypeName) || 0;\n        const anchor = occurrenceCount === 0\n          ? slugify(baseTypeName)\n          : `${slugify(baseTypeName)}-${occurrenceCount + 1}`;\n        const typeDisplay = shouldLink\n          ? `[\\`${displayTypeName}\\`](#${anchor})`\n          : `\\`${typeName}\\``;\n        const desc = cleanDescription(getCommentText(param.comment?.summary), true);\n        mdx += `| ${param.name} | ${typeDisplay} | ${desc} |\\n`;\n      }\n      mdx += `\\n`;\n    }\n\n    // Nest parameter type definitions under this method\n    if (sig.parameters) {\n      for (const param of sig.parameters) {\n        const typeName = getTypeString(param.type);\n        const baseTypeName = typeName.split('\u003c')[0].split(' ')[0].replace(/\\\\?\\|/g, '').trim();\n        // Nest if it's in the registry, not a generic, and not a primitive\n        if (typeRegistry.has(baseTypeName) \u0026\u0026 !isGenericType(baseTypeName) \u0026\u0026 !isPrimitiveType(baseTypeName)) {\n          const typeInfo = typeRegistry.get(baseTypeName);\n          mdx += generateNestedTypeDefinition(typeInfo, baseTypeName, method.name);\n          nestedTypes.add(baseTypeName); // Track that this type was nested\n          // Track occurrence for anchor generation\n          typeOccurrences.set(baseTypeName, (typeOccurrences.get(baseTypeName) || 0) + 1);\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Returns section with nested return type definition\n    if (sig.type) {\n      const returnType = getTypeString(sig.type);\n      // Extract return type without Promise wrapper\n      const unwrappedReturn = returnType.replace(/^Promise\u003c(.+)\u003e$/, '$1');\n\n      if (returnType !== 'void' \u0026\u0026 returnType !== 'Promise') {\n        // Only create link if the type exists in registry\n        const shouldLink = typeRegistry \u0026\u0026 typeRegistry.has(unwrappedReturn) \u0026\u0026 !isGenericType(unwrappedReturn);\n        // Calculate the occurrence number for this type\n        const occurrenceCount = typeOccurrences.get(unwrappedReturn) || 0;\n        const anchor = occurrenceCount === 0\n          ? slugify(unwrappedReturn)\n          : `${slugify(unwrappedReturn)}-${occurrenceCount + 1}`;\n        const returnDisplay = shouldLink\n          ? `[${returnType}](#${anchor})`\n          : returnType;\n        mdx += `**Returns**\\n\\n`;\n        mdx += `${returnDisplay}\\n\\n`;\n\n        // Nest return type definition under this method\n        if (shouldLink \u0026\u0026 isMethodResult(unwrappedReturn)) {\n          const typeInfo = typeRegistry.get(unwrappedReturn);\n          mdx += generateNestedTypeDefinition(typeInfo, unwrappedReturn, method.name);\n          nestedTypes.add(unwrappedReturn); // Track that this type was nested\n          // Track occurrence for anchor generation\n          typeOccurrences.set(unwrappedReturn, (typeOccurrences.get(unwrappedReturn) || 0) + 1);\n        }\n      } else if (returnType !== 'void') {\n        mdx += `**Returns**\\n\\n`;\n        mdx += `${returnType}\\n\\n`;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Examples\n    const examples = getExamples(sig);\n    if (examples.length \u003e 0) {\n      const exampleLabel = examples.length \u003e 1 ? 'Usage Examples' : 'Usage Example';\n      mdx += `**${exampleLabel}**\\n\\n`;\n      examples.forEach(example =\u003e {\n        mdx += `\\`\\`\\`typescript\\n${example}\\n\\`\\`\\`\\n\\n`;\n      });\n    }\n\n    mdx += `---\\n\\n`;\n  }\n\n  return mdx;\n}\n\nfunction generateTypeSections(typeRegistry, nestedTypes) {\n  let mdx = '';\n\n  // Only collect supporting types (params and results are now nested under methods)\n  const supportingTypes = [];\n\n  for (const [name, typeInfo] of typeRegistry.entries()) {\n    if (name === 'AppKitConfig') {\n      continue; // Already documented in AppKit Class section\n    }\n\n    // Skip types that were nested under methods\n    if (nestedTypes.has(name)) {\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Skip generic types (except Promise, but Promise won't be in registry anyway)\n    if (isGenericType(name)) {\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    supportingTypes.push([name, typeInfo]);\n  }\n\n  // Generate supporting types section\n  if (supportingTypes.length \u003e 0) {\n    mdx += `## Supporting Types\\n\\n`;\n    for (const [name, typeInfo] of supportingTypes) {\n      mdx += generateTypeDefinition(typeInfo, name);\n    }\n  }\n\n  return mdx;\n}\n\nfunction generateTypeDefinition(typeInfo, name) {\n  let mdx = `### ${name}\\n\\n`;\n\n  // Description\n  const desc = cleanDescription(getCommentText(typeInfo.comment?.summary));\n  if (desc) {\n    mdx += `${desc}\\n\\n`;\n  }\n\n  // Type signature\n  mdx += `\\`\\`\\`typescript\\n`;\n  if (typeInfo.kind === 256) { // Interface\n    mdx += `interface ${name} {\\n`;\n    if (typeInfo.children) {\n      for (const child of typeInfo.children) {\n        const propType = child.type ? getTypeString(child.type) : 'any';\n        const optional = child.flags?.isOptional ? '?' : '';\n        mdx += `  ${child.name}${optional}: ${propType}\\n`;\n      }\n    }\n    mdx += `}\\n`;\n  } else if (typeInfo.kind === 8) { // Enum\n    mdx += `enum ${name} {\\n`;\n    if (typeInfo.children) {\n      for (const child of typeInfo.children) {\n        // Enums have string or number values\n        const enumValue = child.defaultValue || `'${child.name}'`;\n        mdx += `  ${child.name} = ${enumValue}\\n`;\n      }\n    }\n    mdx += `}\\n`;\n  } else if (typeInfo.kind === 2097152) { // Type alias\n    // Check if this is a re-exported interface (has children but no type property)\n    if (!typeInfo.type \u0026\u0026 typeInfo.children) {\n      // This is likely a re-exported interface, render as interface\n      mdx += `interface ${name} {\\n`;\n      for (const child of typeInfo.children) {\n        const propType = child.type ? getTypeString(child.type) : 'any';\n        const optional = child.flags?.isOptional ? '?' : '';\n        mdx += `  ${child.name}${optional}: ${propType}\\n`;\n      }\n      mdx += `}\\n`;\n    } else if (typeInfo.type) {\n      // Try to expand type alias\n      const expandedType = expandTypeAlias(typeInfo.type);\n      // Check if this is an enum-like union type (has many literal string types)\n      const isEnumLike = typeInfo.type.type === 'union' \u0026\u0026\n                         typeInfo.type.types?.length \u003e 10 \u0026\u0026\n                         typeInfo.type.types.every(t =\u003e t.type === 'literal' || t.type === 'intrinsic');\n\n      if (isEnumLike) {\n        // For enum-like types, just show ellipsis\n        mdx += `type ${name} = ...\\n`;\n      } else {\n        mdx += `type ${name} = ${expandedType}\\n`;\n      }\n    } else {\n      mdx += `type ${name} = ...\\n`;\n    }\n  } else {\n    mdx += `type ${name} = ...\\n`;\n  }\n  mdx += `\\`\\`\\`\\n\\n`;\n\n  // For enum-like unions (type aliases with many values), list the values\n  const isEnumLikeUnion = typeInfo.kind === 2097152 \u0026\u0026\n                          typeInfo.type?.type === 'union' \u0026\u0026\n                          typeInfo.type.types?.length \u003e 10;\n\n  if (isEnumLikeUnion \u0026\u0026 typeInfo.type?.types) {\n    // Determine the label based on the type name\n    let label = 'Supported values';\n    if (name.toLowerCase().includes('blockchain') || name.toLowerCase().includes('chain')) {\n      label = name.toLowerCase().includes('bridge') ? 'Supported chains' : 'Supported blockchains';\n    }\n\n    mdx += `**${label}**\\n\\n`;\n    const values = typeInfo.type.types.map(t =\u003e {\n      if (t.type === 'literal' \u0026\u0026 typeof t.value === 'string') {\n        return `\\`${t.value}\\``;\n      }\n      return `\\`${getTypeString(t)}\\``;\n    }).join(', ');\n    mdx += `${values}\\n\\n`;\n  }\n\n  // For actual enums, list the values\n  if (typeInfo.kind === 8 \u0026\u0026 typeInfo.children) {\n    mdx += `**Values**\\n\\n`;\n    const values = typeInfo.children.map(child =\u003e `\\`${child.name}\\``).join(', ');\n    mdx += `${values}\\n\\n`;\n  }\n\n  // Properties table if it has children (but NOT for enum-like unions or actual enums)\n\n  // Also check if all children are literal types (enum pattern)\n  const hasEnumLikeChildren = typeInfo.children?.every(child =\u003e\n    child.type?.type === 'literal' || child.type?.type === 'intrinsic'\n  );\n\n  // Don't show properties table for enums or enum-like types\n  const isActualEnum = typeInfo.kind === 8;\n\n  if (typeInfo.children \u0026\u0026 typeInfo.children.length \u003e 0 \u0026\u0026 !isEnumLikeUnion \u0026\u0026 !hasEnumLikeChildren \u0026\u0026 !isActualEnum) {\n    mdx += `**Properties**\\n\\n`;\n    mdx += `| Name         | Type                                    | Description                                                                                                                                      |\\n`;\n    mdx += `| ------------ | --------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |\\n`;\n    for (const child of typeInfo.children) {\n      const propType = child.type ? getTypeString(child.type) : 'unknown';\n      // Wrap in backticks if it contains angle brackets, pipes, or quotes to prevent MDX parsing issues\n      const displayType = (propType.includes('\u003c') || propType.includes('\\\\|') || propType.includes(\"'\")) ? `\\`${propType}\\`` : propType;\n      const propDesc = cleanDescription(getCommentText(child.comment?.summary), true);\n      mdx += `| ${child.name} | ${displayType} | ${propDesc} |\\n`;\n    }\n    mdx += `\\n`;\n  }\n\n  mdx += `---\\n\\n`;\n  return mdx;\n}\n\nfunction generateEventTypes(appKit) {\n  let mdx = `## Event Types\\n\\n`;\n  mdx += `### Bridge Events\\n\\n`;\n  mdx += `Bridge events are emitted for each provider in the kit. Events for the built-in\\n`;\n  mdx += `CCTP provider follow its transaction steps. You can subscribe to each event\\n`;\n  mdx += `multiple times with different callbacks.\\n\\n`;\n  mdx += `Bridge events are prefixed with \\`bridge.\\` to namespace them within AppKit:\\n\\n`;\n  mdx += `| Event                | Description                                  |\\n`;\n  mdx += `| -------------------- | -------------------------------------------- |\\n`;\n  mdx += `| \\`bridge.approve\\`     | Token approval transaction completed         |\\n`;\n  mdx += `| \\`bridge.burn\\`        | Source chain burn transaction completed      |\\n`;\n  mdx += `| \\`bridge.attestation\\` | CCTP attestation received                    |\\n`;\n  mdx += `| \\`bridge.mint\\`        | Destination chain mint transaction completed |\\n`;\n  mdx += `| \\`*\\`                  | Wildcard listener for all events             |\\n\\n`;\n\n  // Add on() method documentation reference\n  const onMethod = appKit.children?.find(c =\u003e c.name === 'on');\n  if (onMethod?.signatures?.[0]) {\n    const examples = getExamples(onMethod.signatures[0]);\n    if (examples.length \u003e 0) {\n      const exampleLabel = examples.length \u003e 1 ? 'Usage Examples' : 'Usage Example';\n      mdx += `**${exampleLabel}**\\n\\n`;\n      examples.forEach(example =\u003e {\n        mdx += `\\`\\`\\`typescript\\n${example}\\n\\`\\`\\`\\n\\n`;\n      });\n    }\n  }\n\n  return mdx;\n}\n\nfunction generateUnifiedBalanceSection(ubClass, typeRegistry, nestedTypes) {\n  const methods = ubClass.children?.filter(c =\u003e c.kind === 2048 \u0026\u0026 !c.flags?.isPrivate) || [];\n  let mdx = generateMethods(methods, typeRegistry, nestedTypes, 'kit.unifiedBalance Methods');\n\n  // Prepend the orientation sentence after the section heading\n  mdx = mdx.replace(\n    '## kit.unifiedBalance Methods\\n\\n',\n    '## kit.unifiedBalance Methods\\n\\n' +\n    '`unifiedBalance` is a property on every `AppKit` instance. ' +\n    'Call these methods as `kit.unifiedBalance.methodName()`.\\n\\n'\n  );\n\n  return mdx;\n}\n\nfunction collectTypesFromClass(classNode, typeRegistry, project) {\n  // Get methods\n  const methods = classNode.children?.filter(c =\u003e c.kind === 2048) || [];\n\n  for (const method of methods) {\n    const sig = method.signatures?.[0];\n    if (!sig) continue;\n\n    // Collect parameter types\n    if (sig.parameters) {\n      for (const param of sig.parameters) {\n        collectTypeReferences(param.type, typeRegistry, project);\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Collect return type\n    if (sig.type) {\n      collectTypeReferences(sig.type, typeRegistry, project);\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Also collect AppKitConfig and DeveloperFeeHooks\n  const config = findByNameAndKind(project, 'AppKitConfig', 2097152);\n  if (config) typeRegistry.set('AppKitConfig', config);\n\n  const hooks = findByName(project, 'DeveloperFeeHooks');\n  if (hooks) typeRegistry.set('DeveloperFeeHooks', hooks);\n}\n\nfunction collectTypeReferences(type, typeRegistry, project, depth = 0) {\n  if (!type || depth \u003e 10) return; // Prevent infinite recursion\n\n  if (type.type === 'reference' \u0026\u0026 type.name) {\n    // Found a type reference, try to resolve it\n    if (!typeRegistry.has(type.name)) {\n      const typeNode = findByName(project, type.name);\n      if (typeNode) {\n        typeRegistry.set(type.name, typeNode);\n\n        // Recursively collect types from this type's children (interface/class properties)\n        if (typeNode.children) {\n          for (const child of typeNode.children) {\n            if (child.type) {\n              collectTypeReferences(child.type, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n            }\n          }\n        }\n\n        // For type aliases, collect from the type itself\n        if (typeNode.type) {\n          collectTypeReferences(typeNode.type, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n        }\n\n        // If this is an interface/class with signatures (methods), collect from those too\n        if (typeNode.signatures) {\n          for (const sig of typeNode.signatures) {\n            if (sig.type) {\n              collectTypeReferences(sig.type, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n            }\n            if (sig.parameters) {\n              for (const param of sig.parameters) {\n                if (param.type) {\n                  collectTypeReferences(param.type, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n                }\n              }\n            }\n          }\n        }\n      }\n    } else {\n      // Even if we've seen this type before, still traverse its type arguments\n      const existingTypeNode = typeRegistry.get(type.name);\n      if (existingTypeNode \u0026\u0026 depth \u003c 10) {\n        // Make sure we collect nested types from already-registered types\n        if (existingTypeNode.children) {\n          for (const child of existingTypeNode.children) {\n            if (child.type) {\n              collectTypeReferences(child.type, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n            }\n          }\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Also collect generic type arguments (e.g., Promise\u003cBridgeResult\u003e)\n    if (type.typeArguments) {\n      for (const typeArg of type.typeArguments) {\n        collectTypeReferences(typeArg, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Handle arrays, unions, etc.\n  if (type.type === 'array' \u0026\u0026 type.elementType) {\n    collectTypeReferences(type.elementType, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n  }\n\n  if (type.type === 'union' \u0026\u0026 type.types) {\n    for (const unionType of type.types) {\n      collectTypeReferences(unionType, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (type.type === 'intersection' \u0026\u0026 type.types) {\n    for (const intersectionType of type.types) {\n      collectTypeReferences(intersectionType, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (type.type === 'reflection' \u0026\u0026 type.declaration) {\n    // Collect from reflection's children (inline object properties)\n    if (type.declaration.children) {\n      for (const child of type.declaration.children) {\n        if (child.type) {\n          collectTypeReferences(child.type, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    // Collect from reflection's signatures (inline function types)\n    if (type.declaration.signatures) {\n      for (const sig of type.declaration.signatures) {\n        if (sig.type) {\n          collectTypeReferences(sig.type, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n        }\n        if (sig.parameters) {\n          for (const param of sig.parameters) {\n            if (param.type) {\n              collectTypeReferences(param.type, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n            }\n          }\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Handle indexed access types (e.g., SomeType['key'])\n  if (type.type === 'indexedAccess') {\n    if (type.objectType) {\n      collectTypeReferences(type.objectType, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n    }\n    if (type.indexType) {\n      collectTypeReferences(type.indexType, typeRegistry, project, depth + 1);\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nfunction isMethodParam(name) {\n  return name.endsWith('Params') ||\n         name.endsWith('Config') ||\n         name.endsWith('Context') ||\n         name.endsWith('Destination') ||\n         name === 'CustomFee' ||\n         name === 'AdapterContext';\n}\n\nfunction isMethodResult(name) {\n  return name.endsWith('Result') ||\n         name.endsWith('Estimate') ||\n         name.endsWith('Step') ||\n         name.endsWith('Gas') ||\n         name === 'EstimatedGas';\n}\n\nfunction isGenericType(name) {\n  // List of generic type names to exclude (except Promise which we keep)\n  const genericTypes = [\n    'T', 'K', 'V', 'U', 'E', // Single letter generics\n    'TCapabilities', 'TFromAdapterCapabilities', 'TToAdapterCapabilities',\n    'AdapterCapabilities', 'Capabilities',\n    'Partial', 'Pick', 'Omit', 'Record', 'Exclude', 'Extract', 'Required', 'Readonly'\n  ];\n  return genericTypes.includes(name);\n}\n\nfunction isPrimitiveType(name) {\n  // Primitive types that shouldn't be nested\n  const primitives = [\n    'string', 'number', 'boolean', 'void', 'null', 'undefined', 'any', 'unknown', 'never'\n  ];\n  return primitives.includes(name);\n}\n\nfunction generateNestedTypeDefinition(typeInfo, name, methodName) {\n  let mdx = `#### ${name}\\n\\n`;\n\n  // Description\n  const desc = cleanDescription(getCommentText(typeInfo.comment?.summary));\n  if (desc) {\n    mdx += `${desc}\\n\\n`;\n  }\n\n  // Type signature\n  mdx += `\\`\\`\\`typescript\\n`;\n  if (typeInfo.kind === 256) { // Interface\n    mdx += `interface ${name} {\\n`;\n    if (typeInfo.children) {\n      for (const child of typeInfo.children) {\n        const propType = child.type ? getTypeString(child.type) : 'any';\n        const optional = child.flags?.isOptional ? '?' : '';\n        mdx += `  ${child.name}${optional}: ${propType}\\n`;\n      }\n    }\n    mdx += `}\\n`;\n  } else if (typeInfo.kind === 8) { // Enum\n    mdx += `enum ${name} {\\n`;\n    if (typeInfo.children) {\n      for (const child of typeInfo.children) {\n        const enumValue = child.defaultValue || `'${child.name}'`;\n        mdx += `  ${child.name} = ${enumValue}\\n`;\n      }\n    }\n    mdx += `}\\n`;\n  } else if (typeInfo.kind === 2097152) { // Type alias\n    if (!typeInfo.type \u0026\u0026 typeInfo.children) {\n      mdx += `interface ${name} {\\n`;\n      for (const child of typeInfo.children) {\n        const propType = child.type ? getTypeString(child.type) : 'any';\n        const optional = child.flags?.isOptional ? '?' : '';\n        mdx += `  ${child.name}${optional}: ${propType}\\n`;\n      }\n      mdx += `}\\n`;\n    } else if (typeInfo.type) {\n      const expandedType = expandTypeAlias(typeInfo.type);\n      const isEnumLike = typeInfo.type.type === 'union' \u0026\u0026\n                         typeInfo.type.types?.length \u003e 10 \u0026\u0026\n                         typeInfo.type.types.every(t =\u003e t.type === 'literal' || t.type === 'intrinsic');\n\n      if (isEnumLike) {\n        mdx += `type ${name} = ...\\n`;\n      } else {\n        mdx += `type ${name} = ${expandedType}\\n`;\n      }\n    } else {\n      mdx += `type ${name} = ...\\n`;\n    }\n  } else {\n    mdx += `type ${name} = ...\\n`;\n  }\n  mdx += `\\`\\`\\`\\n\\n`;\n\n  // Properties table if applicable\n  const hasEnumLikeChildren = typeInfo.children?.every(child =\u003e\n    child.type?.type === 'literal' || child.type?.type === 'intrinsic'\n  );\n  const isActualEnum = typeInfo.kind === 8;\n  const isEnumLikeUnion = typeInfo.kind === 2097152 \u0026\u0026\n                          typeInfo.type?.type === 'union' \u0026\u0026\n                          typeInfo.type.types?.length \u003e 10;\n\n  if (typeInfo.children \u0026\u0026 typeInfo.children.length \u003e 0 \u0026\u0026 !isEnumLikeUnion \u0026\u0026 !hasEnumLikeChildren \u0026\u0026 !isActualEnum) {\n    mdx += `**Properties**\\n\\n`;\n    mdx += `| Name         | Type                                    | Description                                                                                                                                      |\\n`;\n    mdx += `| ------------ | --------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |\\n`;\n    for (const child of typeInfo.children) {\n      const propType = child.type ? getTypeString(child.type) : 'unknown';\n      // Strip generics from property types for cleaner table display\n      const baseType = propType.split('\u003c')[0].trim();\n      const displayType = (propType.includes('\u003c') || propType.includes('\\\\|') || propType.includes(\"'\")) ? `\\`${baseType}\\`` : propType;\n      const propDesc = cleanDescription(getCommentText(child.comment?.summary), true);\n      mdx += `| ${child.name} | ${displayType} | ${propDesc} |\\n`;\n    }\n    mdx += `\\n`;\n  }\n\n  return mdx;\n}\n\nfunction getExamples(signature) {\n  if (!signature?.comment?.blockTags) return [];\n\n  return signature.comment.blockTags\n    .filter(tag =\u003e tag.tag === '@example')\n    .map(tag =\u003e {\n      const text = tag.content.map(c =\u003e c.text).join('');\n      return text.replace(/^```typescript\\s*\\n?/,'').replace(/\\n?```$/,'').trim();\n    });\n}\n\nfunction getCommentText(summaryArray) {\n  if (!summaryArray) return '';\n  // Preserve line breaks in the comment text\n  return summaryArray.map(s =\u003e s.text).join('').trim();\n}\n\nfunction cleanDescription(text, inTable = false) {\n  if (!text) return '';\n\n  // Remove orphan type names on their own line (from @interface, @type tags in JSDoc)\n  text = text.replace(/^\\s*\\b[A-Z][a-zA-Z0-9_\u003c\u003e]+\\s*$/gm, '');\n\n  // Strip bold FIRST (before italic) so **word** doesn't leave stray single *\n  // that the italic regex partially matches (e.g. **term** → *term* → _term_).\n  text = text.replace(/\\*\\*([^*]+)\\*\\*/g, '$1');\n\n  // Strip single-asterisk italic markers (*word* and _word_) — TypeDoc emits\n  // both and Prettier converts *word* → _word_ which fails MD049 in CI.\n  text = text.replace(/\\*([^*\\n]+)\\*/g, '$1');\n  text = text.replace(/(?\u003c!\\w)_([^_\\n]+)_(?!\\w)/g, '$1');\n\n  // Replace single quotes with backticks for code, but not inside existing backtick spans\n  // (prevents turning 'CONFIRMED' inside `forwardState === 'CONFIRMED'` into a broken span)\n  const backtickSpans = [];\n  text = text.replace(/`[^`]+`/g, match =\u003e {\n    backtickSpans.push(match);\n    return `___BTSPAN${backtickSpans.length - 1}___`;\n  });\n  text = text.replace(/'([^'\\s]+(?:\\s+[^'\\s]+)?)'(?!s\\b)/g, '`$1`');\n  text = text.replace(/___BTSPAN(\\d+)___/g, (_, i) =\u003e backtickSpans[Number(i)]);\n\n  // Replace \"cross-chain\" with \"crosschain\" EXCEPT for \"Cross-Chain Transfer Protocol\" (CCTP's official name)\n  // First, temporarily mark CCTP's official name, then replace other instances, then restore it\n  text = text.replace(/Cross-Chain Transfer Protocol \\(CCTP\\)/gi, '___CCTP_OFFICIAL_NAME___');\n  text = text.replace(/cross-chain/gi, 'crosschain');\n  text = text.replace(/___CCTP_OFFICIAL_NAME___/g, 'Cross-Chain Transfer Protocol (CCTP)');\n  text = text.replace(/single-chain/gi, 'same-chain');\n\n  // Wrap technical terms in code font (avoid double-wrapping already backticked terms)\n  text = text.replace(/\\b(traceId|kitKey|allowanceStrategy|slippageBps|txHash|invocationMeta)(?!`)\\b/g, '`$1`');\n\n  // Escape pipe characters that would break tables\n  text = text.replace(/\\|/g, '\\\\|');\n\n  if (inTable) {\n    // For table cells, handle bullet lists and paragraphs specially\n    // First, mark paragraph breaks (double newlines) as special markers\n    text = text.replace(/\\n\\n+/g, ' ___PARAGRAPH_BREAK___ ');\n    // Replace bullet list markers with \u003cbr/\u003e for line breaks in tables\n    // Keep the dash for the bullet point visual\n    text = text.replace(/^\\s*[-*+]\\s+/gm, '\u003cbr/\u003e- ');\n    // Replace remaining single newlines with spaces\n    text = text.replace(/\\n/g, ' ');\n    // Convert paragraph breaks to \u003cbr/\u003e\u003cbr/\u003e\n    text = text.replace(/___PARAGRAPH_BREAK___/g, '\u003cbr/\u003e\u003cbr/\u003e');\n    // Clean up multiple spaces\n    text = text.replace(/\\s+/g, ' ');\n    // Clean up space before \u003cbr/\u003e but not after (to preserve list formatting)\n    text = text.replace(/\\s+\u003cbr\\/\u003e/g, '\u003cbr/\u003e');\n    // Clean up leading \u003cbr/\u003e at the start (shouldn't start with line break)\n    text = text.replace(/^\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\s*/, '');\n  } else {\n    // For non-table content, preserve some structure\n    // Clean up multiple spaces BUT preserve newlines\n    text = text.replace(/[^\\S\\n]+/g, ' ');\n    // Trim each line\n    text = text.split('\\n').map(line =\u003e line.trim()).join('\\n');\n    // Remove excess newlines (more than 2 consecutive)\n    text = text.replace(/\\n{3,}/g, '\\n\\n');\n  }\n\n  // Remove any double backticks that may have been created\n  text = text.replace(/``+/g, '`');\n\n  return text.trim();\n}\n\nfunction expandTypeAlias(type) {\n  if (!type) return 'unknown';\n\n  if (type.type === 'intersection') {\n    // For intersections, try to expand reflections inline\n    const parts = type.types.map(t =\u003e {\n      if (t.type === 'reflection' \u0026\u0026 t.declaration?.children) {\n        // Expand the inline object type\n        const props = t.declaration.children.map(child =\u003e {\n          const propType = child.type ? getTypeString(child.type) : 'any';\n          const optional = child.flags?.isOptional ? '?' : '';\n          return `${child.name}${optional}: ${propType}`;\n        }).join(', ');\n        return `{ ${props} }`;\n      }\n      return getTypeString(t);\n    });\n    return parts.join(' \u0026 ');\n  }\n\n  if (type.type === 'union') {\n    // Don't expand very long unions (like enums)\n    if (type.types.length \u003e 10) {\n      return '...'; // Enum-like unions\n    }\n    return type.types.map(t =\u003e getTypeString(t)).join(' | ');\n  }\n\n  if (type.type === 'reflection') {\n    return '{ ... }';\n  }\n\n  return getTypeString(type);\n}\n\nfunction findByNameAndKind(project, name, kind) {\n  return findByNameAndKindRecursive(project, name, kind);\n}\n\nfunction findByNameAndKindRecursive(node, name, kind) {\n  if (node.name === name \u0026\u0026 node.kind === kind) {\n    return node;\n  }\n\n  if (node.children) {\n    for (const child of node.children) {\n      const found = findByNameAndKindRecursive(child, name, kind);\n      if (found) return found;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return null;\n}\n\nfunction findByName(project, name) {\n  return findByNameRecursive(project, name);\n}\n\nfunction findByNameRecursive(node, name) {\n  if (node.name === name) {\n    return node;\n  }\n\n  if (node.children) {\n    for (const child of node.children) {\n      const found = findByNameRecursive(child, name);\n      if (found) return found;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return null;\n}\n\nfunction getTypeString(type) {\n  if (!type) return 'void';\n\n  if (type.type === 'intrinsic') {\n    return type.name;\n  }\n\n  if (type.type === 'literal') {\n    // Handle string literals (e.g., 'Ethereum', 'USDC')\n    if (typeof type.value === 'string') {\n      return `'${type.value}'`;\n    }\n    return String(type.value);\n  }\n\n  if (type.type === 'reference') {\n    // Handle Promise\u003cT\u003e - extract the T\n    if (type.name === 'Promise' \u0026\u0026 type.typeArguments \u0026\u0026 type.typeArguments.length \u003e 0) {\n      return getTypeString(type.typeArguments[0]);\n    }\n    // Handle generic types like Partial\u003cT\u003e, Record\u003cK, V\u003e, etc.\n    if (type.typeArguments \u0026\u0026 type.typeArguments.length \u003e 0) {\n      const args = type.typeArguments.map(t =\u003e getTypeString(t)).join(', ');\n      return `${type.name}\u003c${args}\u003e`;\n    }\n    return type.name;\n  }\n\n  if (type.type === 'array') {\n    return `${getTypeString(type.elementType)}[]`;\n  }\n\n  if (type.type === 'union') {\n    // Don't expand very long unions (like enums with 30+ values)\n    if (type.types.length \u003e 10) {\n      return '...'; // Will be handled by caller\n    }\n    return type.types.map(t =\u003e getTypeString(t)).join(' \\\\| ');\n  }\n\n  if (type.type === 'reflection' \u0026\u0026 type.declaration?.signatures) {\n    const sig = type.declaration.signatures[0];\n    const params = sig.parameters?.map(p =\u003e `${p.name}: ${getTypeString(p.type)}`).join(', ') || '';\n    const ret = getTypeString(sig.type);\n    return `(${params}) =\u003e ${ret}`;\n  }\n\n  if (type.type === 'reflection') {\n    return 'object';\n  }\n\n  return 'any';\n}\n\nfunction slugify(text) {\n  return text.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '');\n}\n\n// Run the generator\ngenerateDocs();\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"43:[\"$\",\"$L4a\",null,{\"customJsDisabled\":false,\"jsFiles\":[{\"_id\":\"691229eea47d8ee61851cc44\",\"filePath\":\"disclaimer-injector.js\",\"subdomain\":\"arc-docs\",\"__v\":0,\"content\":\"$4b\"},{\"_id\":\"69cfe6db16a632c444b89e3b\",\"filePath\":\"scripts/generate_sdk_reference.js\",\"subdomain\":\"arc-docs\",\"__v\":0,\"content\":\"$4c\"}]}]\n4f:T7239,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"\"use
